\subsection{Detailed Description}
Stores all of the settings for the supported fixed configurations. {\bfseries Description} Stores all of the settings for the fixed configurations. The settings are for the start data, stop data, as well as the buffer requirements. 

Definition in file \hyperlink{_fixed_config_settings_8h_source}{Fixed\-Config\-Settings.\-h}.
